## Text Elements
Research question:

- How can interaction with non-human agents
    inform our relationship digital systems?
- How does the presence of a non-human agent 
    affect our experience qualitatively? 
 ^2SyI2S6k

early digital systems
neural representation
emergence of new media ^s0XwXNj1

diff uses of ML
user/viewer experience
format/concept for installation ^xC0gIZuG

TD Neuron
Preempting motion  ^RSJfuJeN

III. ML Training
- Using program TD Neuron which will be trained live by participant interaction
 ^2wGVITis

IV. Installation
- Large room to facilitate movement
- Visible cameras for video stream
 ^D5OOeFC3

Project will culminate in a research paper and an installation

The paper will contain:
- An introduction on cybernetics: 
    - Historical background on the early metaphorical descriptions of ANNs and the 
        interdisciplinary thought that led to the creation of NNs as we know them
        - Postmodern 
- An introduction on digital art: 
    - An overview of how artists began to represent digital relationships; 
        visualizations of the digital
- Specific examples of ANNs/ML in contemporary art
    - Amber Frid-Jimenez
    - Marco Barotti
- Concluding: why is this valuable to cognitive science?
    - A philosophical analysis of the value of images and how metaphor shapes 
    our understanding of AI  ^Qoray3nY

The paper serves to contextualize and support the installation as a work in the field of cognitive science. 
The installation is the  ^EcLaOGbA
